{"kind": "blogger#postList", "nextPageToken": "CgkIChiE5rqrpycQy4Ca9ZL8nrwx", "items": [{"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "4699611095287704520", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2012-11-01T09:29:00+05:30", "updated": "2014-09-13T11:18:10+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNDEwNTg3MjkwNjg4Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2012/10/the-joy-of-having-cat-as-pet-capt-ajit.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/4699611095287704520", "title": "THE JOY OF HAVING A CAT AS A PET-  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-JvoJLvqFnx4/UJJ30WIX0VI/AAAAAAAAWfQ/mH06Nl49Kq0/s1600/jhhhh.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-JvoJLvqFnx4/UJJ30WIX0VI/AAAAAAAAWfQ/mH06Nl49Kq0/s400/jhhhh.jpg\" height=\"299\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<b><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><br /></span></b>\n<b><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">THE JOY OF HAVING A CAT AS A PET</span></b> - &nbsp;CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WaUnDUfyBho/UKhuK8szyaI/AAAAAAAAYhQ/cBn0UukNcKs/s1600/430678_10151323728724343_1433993657_n.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WaUnDUfyBho/UKhuK8szyaI/AAAAAAAAYhQ/cBn0UukNcKs/s400/430678_10151323728724343_1433993657_n.jpg\" height=\"400\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cats are\nunderestimated. They can learn complex tasks, especially if the reward is food.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In highly structured\ntests of learning ability, cats often outperformed dogs in the ability to\nmaster conceptual problems.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cat's have the ability\nto master \"oddity learning\" in which the animal is shown three\nobjects and is rewarded for selecting the one that is most unlike the other\ntwo. In the test, cats learned to paw a square block rather than two round\nblocks presented at the same time, because food was hidden beneath the square\nblock.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">They are capable of\nforming attachments to people and communicating their needs and wants. They are\ncapable of \"instinctual thought.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">They have personalities\n- and that may mean that they don't hesitate to demand whatever they want, be\nit food, play, or to be left alone.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">How do cats get our\nattention? Those with louder \"voices\" may meow at their owners\nendlessly. They may also follow you around, insist on sitting on your laps , or\nrub against your ankles. All of these are signs that the cat uses to say\n\"I'm here! Pay attention to me!\"&nbsp;\n<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I saw my cat up on my\ndining room table, trying to eat the fired fish from the top floor . When I\nwalked down the stairs to the dining room, she quickly jumped onto the chair\nthat she usually sleeps on, and pretended she was sleeping!<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">All my three cats know\nhow to open door handles. They know how to press the knob and open the\nmicrowave too.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cats, like humans, have\nbinocular vision that gives them depth perception.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Twice my cats warned my\nwife when a snake came into our compound.&nbsp;\nOnce when it entered our house.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cats are far more\nindependent and can take care of themselves better.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Provide adequate food\nand water and a cat can be left home alone for a few days while you go on\nvacation, dogs can't. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cats have a personality\nare too intelligent to perform on command, unlike dogs who are \u201cfollow the leader\u201d\ntype pack animals.. &nbsp;The solitary cat\nanswers to no one and is motivated by the sole need to survive.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cats have\nexcellent memory, and positive experiences are just as easily stored and\nrecalled, particularly if they have to do with food or play. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Many of them also have an uncanny ability to\nknow the hour of their regular feeding time. &nbsp;They will wake up the sleeping owner by nibbling\non the toes. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Our cats respond to the\nname call by looking into the eyes, with an instant MEOW.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cats can be toilet\ntrained.&nbsp; Outdoors they dig a hole for a\ncrap and cover it up. Indoors they go through the same motions as programmed in\ntheir DNA.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dogs will take a\ncommand, cats do as \"they\" please. Owning a cat is a good forerunner\nof marriage. You learn that you cannot control another living being, or expect\nsomeone to do everything you want.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cats give themselves a\nbath.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cat owners are smarter\nthan dog owners. The purity of a person's heart can be quickly measured by how\nthey regard cats. A cat has absolute emotional honesty, human beings, for one\nreason or another, may hide their feelings, but a cat is not a hypocrite. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">If you are worthy of\nits affection, a cat will be your friend, but never your slave.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is such a joy to see\nthem early in the morning chasing butterflies and squirrels.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I have seen a squirrel\nPLAY DEAD for 3 hours , and then when I shooed my cat away ( who was toying\naround with it with such determination ) , the squirrel just took off like a\nbullet.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; Hemp made uniforms are\nfound to be tougher and more resilient than cotton.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In 1942 U.S. scientists\nworking at the Office of Strategic Services (OSS), manned by Rothschild's\npayroll scientists , (the CIA\u2019s wartime predecessor) ,selected a potent extract\nof marijuana as the best available \"truth serum.\"&nbsp; The cannabis concoction was given the code\nname TD, meaning Truth Drug. The Journal of the American Medical\nAssociation released findings from a 20-year study and analysis of over 5,000\nsmokers showed that cannabis did not harm lung function, although cigarettes did.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Cannabis helps fight inflammation and counteracts the effects of irritating\nchemicals in the drug.&nbsp; The study\nconcluded: \"Occasional and low cumulative marijuana use was not associated\nwith adverse effects on pulmonary function\".<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-If6v30Wpn_Q/UJGUYLCgj_I/AAAAAAAAWY0/RmdhRUptnTA/s1600/images+(1)mnvfr.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-If6v30Wpn_Q/UJGUYLCgj_I/AAAAAAAAWY0/RmdhRUptnTA/s1600/images+(1)mnvfr.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Research done by the Scripps\nResearch Institute in California shows that the active ingredient in marijuana,\nTHC, prevents the formation of deposits in the brain associated with\nAlzheimer's disease. THC was found to prevent an enzyme called\nacetylcholinesterase from accelerating the formation of \"Alzheimer\nplaques\" in the brain more effectively than commercially marketed drugs.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">THC is also more effective at blocking clumps of protein that can inhibit\nmemory and cognition in Alzheimer\u2019s patients, as reported in Molecular\nPharmaceutics. Cannabinoids can also potentially prevent or slow the\nprogression of Alzheimer's disease by reducing tau protein phosphorylation,\noxidative stress, and neuroinflammation.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">According to a 2007 and\na 2010 study at the California Pacific Medical Center Research Institute,\ncannabidiol (CBD) stops breast cancer from spreading throughout the body by\ndownregulating a gene called ID1. This may provide a non-toxic alternative to\nchemotherapy while achieving the same results without the painful and\nunpleasant side effects.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Investigators at\nColumbia University published clinical trial data in 2007 showing that HIV/AIDS\npatients who inhaled cannabis four times daily experienced substantial\nincreases in food intake with little evidence of discomfort and no impairment\nof cognitive performance. They concluded that smoked cannabis has a clear\nmedical benefit in HIV-positive patients.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-BVMF4OaRVKw/UJGT5weaLhI/AAAAAAAAWYc/TpmS6UzzsAk/s1600/images+%25281%2529lkjgrrew.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-BVMF4OaRVKw/UJGT5weaLhI/AAAAAAAAWYc/TpmS6UzzsAk/s320/images+%25281%2529lkjgrrew.jpg\" width=\"310\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In another study in\n2008, researchers at the University of California, San Diego School of Medicine\nfound that marijuana significantly reduces HIV-related neuropathic pain when\nadded to a patient's already-prescribed pain management regimen and may be an\n\"effective option for pain relief\" in those whose pain is not\ncontrolled with current medications. Mood disturbance, physical disability, and\nquality of life all improved significantly during study treatment. &nbsp;It eases essential tremors.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Despite management with\nopioids and other pain modifying therapies, neuropathic pain continues to reduce\nthe quality of life and daily functioning in HIV-infected individuals.\nCannabinoid receptors in the central and peripheral nervous systems have been\nshown to modulate pain perception. No serious adverse effects were reported,\naccording to the study published by the American Academy of Neurology. A study\nexamining the effectiveness of different drugs for HIV associated neuropathic\npain found that smoked Cannabis was one of only three drugs that showed\nevidence of efficacy.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-VU-_oWQF3Bo/UJGUMzCtwEI/AAAAAAAAWYs/jyuGxfoslD0/s1600/images+(1)hjhrew.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">A study by Complutense\nUniversity of Madrid found the chemicals in cannabis promote the death of brain\ncancer cells by essentially helping them feed upon themselves in a process\ncalled autophagy.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Smoking marijuana\nshortly after having a stroke prevents the swelling of the brain -- and consequently\nmuch of the brain damage and loss of function associated with strokes. pot has\nabsolutely no toxicity to human tissues; pot has anti-carcinogenic properties;\nthe tar, although greater in proportion than tobacco, is completely\nwater-soluble. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-j7xRDedfc7o/UJGVWT3juOI/AAAAAAAAWZc/WE2yWpoEnhQ/s1600/images+(1)bhuu.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hemp is a dioecious,\nwoody, herbaceous annual. Each short growing season it reaches heights of\ntwelve to twenty feet, and grows well in any climate or soil condition. Its\nroots penetrate deep (one foot per month), breaking up compacted and overworked\nsoil, and combating soil erosion. Since it grows so quickly, it could be a year\nround crop, harvested twice a year, or it could be planted as a second crop,\nafter harvest of a different one. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This willing plant is\nable to provide many basic needs of humans anywhere on the planet: food,\nmedicine, treeless shelter and paper, clothing and other textiles, and a\nrenewable fuel alternative to those presently creating acid rain, global\nwarming, and deforestation. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">One acre of hemp\nprovides the same amount of cellulose and fiber pulp, used to make paper\nproducts and pressed or particleboard, as four acres of trees, while producing\nfour to seven times less pollution. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; Rivers could recover from paper industry chemicals.\n<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Nutrition wise, hemp\nseed is the highest in essential fatty acids and the lowest in saturated fats.\nIt can be made into a tofu-like curd at a cheaper cost than can soya, sprouted\nto make milk and ice cream or for use in salad, ground and used like flour, or\npressed into an oil, whose by-product is a high protein animal feed.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; They are made into a Kanjee\nor soup by boiling with water, mixed with wine ,made into pills, and beaten\ninto a paste.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">These were some reasons\nthe pharmaceutical companies got worried. It is usually consumed as an infusion in beverage\nform, and varies in strength according to how much cannabis is used in the\npreparation. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-jw9cYV9vaGs/UrAfac01hMI/AAAAAAAAoXg/5b3q5E_jZnw/s1600/cannabinoid-society-of-canada-cbd-thc-cbn-cbg-delta-9-endocannbinoid-system-human-health-cannabis-medical-hemp-hearts-seeds-freezeland-medical-cannabis-endocannabinoids1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-jw9cYV9vaGs/UrAfac01hMI/AAAAAAAAoXg/5b3q5E_jZnw/s640/cannabinoid-society-of-canada-cbd-thc-cbn-cbg-delta-9-endocannbinoid-system-human-health-cannabis-medical-hemp-hearts-seeds-freezeland-medical-cannabis-endocannabinoids1.jpg\" width=\"520\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The second, <span style=\"color: blue;\">ganja</span>,\nconsisting of the leaves and the plant tops, is smoked. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The third, called\n<span style=\"color: blue;\">charas or hashish</span>, consists of the resinous buds and/or extracted resin from\nthe leaves of the marijuana plant. The Mercedes C-Class has up to 20 kg\nof hemp in each car.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hemp paper from Russian\nmills were used for bank notes, stamped paper, credit bills, postal stamps,\nbonds, stocks, and other watermarked paper.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hemp paper is stronger\nand less environmentally destructive than paper made of trees.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hemp rope was used in\nthe age of sailing ships, though the rope had to be protected by tarring. Hemp\nrope was phased out when Manila, which does not require tarring, became widely\navailable.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hemp-fibres were also used as part of a caulking that made\nthe hull of sailing ships watertight.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Fk3cbhRiWKM/UJGQHUclCxI/AAAAAAAAWVc/nrw1DCRZgyE/s1600/14658262-hemp-rope-textured-background.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Fk3cbhRiWKM/UJGQHUclCxI/AAAAAAAAWVc/nrw1DCRZgyE/s320/14658262-hemp-rope-textured-background.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Sailors</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;made hemp shoes and baskets. &nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The male plants were\nused for making linen and sails because the fibers are finer then those of the\nfemale plant. Or the coarser fibers of the female were used for making more\nheavy canvas and rope.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-erFjCTCTJAw/UJGOKOXy-nI/AAAAAAAAWUE/0F1LgdaEax0/s1600/images+(1)ygnnjjj.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-erFjCTCTJAw/UJGOKOXy-nI/AAAAAAAAWUE/0F1LgdaEax0/s1600/images+(1)ygnnjjj.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">We sailors know that Hemp\nropes retains more strength when the yarn is twisted to the right. This resulted\nin a left hand strand, and a right hand rope. It wasn't until modern times that\nmicroscopic examination of the plant illustrated that the structure of the\nplant has a natural twist that causes this effect.\" This explains why Left\nHand Strands twisted together as Right Hand lay (\"Z\" twist) make\nstronger hemp rope.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-u2pRhe5uOvE/UJGOBZpjbXI/AAAAAAAAWT8/tdclZpUa2Qg/s1600/130px-Cordage_en_chanvre.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"248\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-u2pRhe5uOvE/UJGOBZpjbXI/AAAAAAAAWT8/tdclZpUa2Qg/s320/130px-Cordage_en_chanvre.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Hemp can be used as a\n\"mop crop\" to clear impurities out of wastewater, such as sewage\neffluent, excessive phosphorus from chicken litter, or other unwanted\nsubstances or chemicals. In addition to over 2,000 hearts, there were a\nlarge number of brain parts, eyes taken from over 15,000 stillborn foetuses and\nperhaps most disturbingly of all, a number of children's heads and bodies.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-I0Y_wj6UeJg/UI-BrbkwARI/AAAAAAAAWQw/he2WUUmyvUU/s1600/imagesU6RT.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-I0Y_wj6UeJg/UI-BrbkwARI/AAAAAAAAWQw/he2WUUmyvUU/s1600/imagesU6RT.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Al Jazeera Magazine referred\nto an international Israeli conspiracy to kidnap children and harvest their\norgans and repeats a Pravda story that Israel has brought some 25,000 Ukrainian\nchildren into the occupied entity over the past two years in order to harvest\ntheir organs. &nbsp;Several Russian and\nUkrainian officers who sailed with me have lost attractive young girls from their\nown circle of friends and acquaintances. One of them was the wife of my own\nthird Russian mate .&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><b><span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span></b></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Xcr07ZVjmbE/UI98BFI1RFI/AAAAAAAAWNw/yxCfsK0Sdl4/s1600/imagesKKUY545.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">An article in the\nAlgerian daily Al-Khabar said that Algerian children were being kidnapped into\nMorocco and sold to Israelis and American Jews to harvest their organs for sale.\n.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IfMeZVPw8b8/UI9_EJkzNpI/AAAAAAAAWPA/wCF9u2xHMZM/s1600/downloadBGGTR.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The donors were from\nMoldova, Kazakhstan, Russia and Turkey and were enticed with the false promise\nof payments as much as 20 thousand dollars. However, they were cheated and never\ngot any money, nor the post operative care.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In February 1992, in Argentina,\nthe minister of health admitted that the director of the Montes de Oca\npsychiatric clinic, located near Buenos Aires, had been taking blood and\norgans, especially corneas, from the patients in the facility. The\ninvestigation still goes on to find out the destination of the organs, as well\nas of the many children born in the establishment. The minister revealed some frightening\nstatistics: between 1986 and 1992, one-thousand three-hundred and twenty-one of\nthese psychiatric patients died. The swamps surrounding the clinic are being\ndragged in an attempt to find out what became of an additional one-thousand\nthree- hundred and ninety-five patients who simply disappeared. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-9zrsfPzPEl4/UI9_IzlGUII/AAAAAAAAWPI/vyLzB9IDlIY/s1600/downloadKUTF.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-9zrsfPzPEl4/UI9_IzlGUII/AAAAAAAAWPI/vyLzB9IDlIY/s1600/downloadKUTF.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">After Argentina, it was\nthe turn of Columbia. At the beginning of March 1992, a chamber of horrors\nreminiscent of Dr. Frankenstein was discovered. The corpses of ten paupers, one\nof them a 15- year-old girl, were found in the amphitheater of Barranquilla Faculty\nof Medicine. The remains of forty other persons had decomposed to the point\nthat they could not be identified. The procedure used by the faculty's security\npatrol had been to strike beggars over the head with baseball bats until the\nvictimsvwere in a state of coma. They were not killed until after their organs\nof commercial value had been extracted, which were sold on the black market.\nWhat remained of the cadavers was then turned over to the medical students for\ndissection purposes, or disposed of in the garbage.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Nu1KL77VRiU/UI-AJ6A7RlI/AAAAAAAAWQA/X6YgaFswNkE/s1600/imagesMJYTRTRE.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Nu1KL77VRiU/UI-AJ6A7RlI/AAAAAAAAWQA/X6YgaFswNkE/s1600/imagesMJYTRTRE.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I own a plot of land\nadjacent to a orphanage cum mental home run by Christian padres.&nbsp; I received a report from my caretaker about\nkidney harvesting in this place.&nbsp; So one\nday I went all the way there, threw a cricket ball into the compound , put a\ntall ladder and jumped over the wall when the inmates were taking a mass bath\nat the well , during bath hour.&nbsp; Some of\nthem ( mental cases ) had the UNMISTAKABLE incision on one side -- used only\nfor kidney removals. It was a living organ bank.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">International organ\ntrafficking has become a huge multibillion dollar business and it continues to\ngrow. The traffickers have become more and more ruthless and have absolutely no\nboundaries. Most of the time they work under patronage of the local police and\npoliticians.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This globally black\nmarket is deceptive and dirty. The traffickers use deception, violence and\ncoercion to buy and sell organs from desperate people and sell them for much\nhigher price to more developed countries. These middlemen form partnership with\ndoctors in different hospitals who perform these transplants for an arranged\nfee and no questions. The profit margin is too high. They will pay 1000 Dollars\nfor a kidney and sell it for 250, 000 dollars. &nbsp;In poor countries victims sleep on the\nstreets.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">-- t</span><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\">he British imported a brainwashed\nGandhi from South Africa, using Gokhale,</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;and planted him in India&nbsp;\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">to sabotage the Indian freedom movement</span> which was snowballing with\nunstoppable fury</span></b></span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">--&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">-- so much that they had to shift the capital from Calcutta to\nDelhi..</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">All of the Indian\nfreedom fighting movement history which you learnt is all a BIG WHITE LIE.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Rothschild&nbsp; sponsored his education in London and he\ntravelled to London in 1874 and returned in 1875. He was brainwashed there at\nMiddle Temple , with Edmund Burke's philosophy.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In 1875 before he came back he founded the crypto freedom fighting\norganisation \"British Indian Association\" whose minutes of the\nmeeting would be read by Rothschild.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Edmund Burke was the\n\"Paymaster of the British forces\" , an exalted treasurer post created\nby Rothschild, the owner of British East India Company. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">After returning to\nIndia he taught English at the the FREE CHURCH.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Before this\nbrainwashing period Rothscild educated Surendra Banerjee in England .&nbsp; His father put him on a ship on 3rd March\n1868, without telling his mother.&nbsp; At\nSouthampton a Rothschild stooge Womesh Chunder Bonnerjee received him.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-XTU8pEKVCwI/UImI08VvMcI/AAAAAAAAVz0/LvC_KrpmDVU/s1600/WCBonnerjee.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-XTU8pEKVCwI/UImI08VvMcI/AAAAAAAAVz0/LvC_KrpmDVU/s320/WCBonnerjee.jpg\" width=\"201\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><b>WC Bannerjee</b> though a\nBrahmin, had converted himself and his family to Christianity, and was later\nthe First President of Indian National Congress at Bombay in 1885. &nbsp; WC was President of INC again in 1892 at Allahabad. &nbsp;Gen JN Chaudhuri , the Chief of Indian Army\nwas his grandson. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Can you believe this ,\nDadabhai Naoroji the Opium agent of Rothschild in England was also one of the\nfounder fathers of the INC, the crypto freedom fighting agency.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dadhabhai Naoroji given\nthe sobriquet of the \"Grand old man of India\"&nbsp; in our school Social studies and History text\nbooks , was in England was 51 years --&nbsp;\nring a bell?&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">We Indians are monkeys,\nright?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In 1879, he founded the\nnewspaper, The Bengalee.&nbsp;&nbsp; In 1883, when\nBanerjee was arrested for publishing remarks in his paper, in contempt of\ncourt, protests and hartals erupted across Bengal, and in Indian cities such as\nAgra, Faizabad, Amritsar, Lahore and Pune&nbsp;\n.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">All this was a sham to get into the hearts of the Indians. The British and Rothschild controlled press did massive propaganda.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Banerjee was a highly\nvocal figure in the Swadeshi movement - advocating goods manufactured in India\nagainst foreign products .&nbsp; He was\narrested for singing Vande Mataram which was banned\u2014all a big sham.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">On 14 April\n1906 Surendranath Banerjee led a huge public procession against that ban in\nBarisal (now in Bangladesh). &nbsp;He was heavily fined for public consumption.&nbsp;&nbsp; - and his popularity at its apex made him ,\nin words of his gullible Bengali admirers, the uncrowned king of Bengal.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Surendranath Banerjee\nsupported the Morley-Minto reforms 1909 \u2013 which were resented by all patriotic\nIndians.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Indian Councils Act 1909 , commonly known as the Morley-Minto\nReforms, was an Act of the Parliament of the United Kingdom that brought about\nthe right of separate electorate for the Indian&nbsp;Muslims , to split the unity of the Indian Freedom movement.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Only Muslims could now vote for candidates\nfor the Muslim seats.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">On 01 July 1909,&nbsp; a great patriot Madan Lal Dhingra\nassassinated Curzon Wylie at a public meeting in London.&nbsp; Surendranath Bannejee sent an open letter\ncondemning Dhingra's actions to the press, and this made the British and\nRothschild very happy.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Surendranath Banerjee\nactively supported the Montagu-Chelmsford reforms (1919 ) where besides\nMuslims, other minorities including Sikhs, Anglo-Indians, Christians and\nEuropeans were also given the right of separate electorate\u2014a blatant divide and\nrule policy. Very few Indians could actually vote.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">He was elected to the\nreformed Legislative Council of Bengal in 1921. &nbsp;He threw caution to the winds,\nand accepted the portfolio of minister in the Bengal government. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\">This earned him the ire of all Indian freedom\nfighters and much of the public.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">He lost the next election to\nthe Bengal Legislative Assembly in 1923 to Bidhan Chandra Roy, the candidate of\nthe Swarajya Party,&nbsp; in a most\nhumiliating manner \u2013 ending his British sponsored political career for all\npractical purposes.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: red; May such things never ever happen to our army .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">VK Krishna Menon was friendly towards Russia and China. The Americans did NOT want India, though non-aligned , to tilt towards the Communists who had broken free from Rothschild brand of Communism.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Rothschild used CIA to provoke the sleeping giant China in a dirty manner and put the blame on India. &nbsp;The CIA financed and armed a major resistance movement inside Tibet during the 1950's.&nbsp; China had long suspected that India was an active but covert party to this movement.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">This subtle declaration of war against China was the culmination of a policy that Nehru had been pursuing since as early as April 1947 when India was still a British colony. &nbsp;On 25 April 1947, the external affairs department of the government of India, of which Nehru was in charge as a member of the viceroy\u2019s \u2018interim government\u2019, &nbsp;informed the British secretary of state for India.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;QUOTE &nbsp;\u201cGovernment of India now wish to be represented in Tibet ( as per Edwina\u2019s advise to Nehru )&nbsp; ... and should be grateful to know whether His Majesty\u2019s Government desire to retain separate Mission there in future. If they do not, it would seem feasible to arrange transition from \u2018British Mission\u2019 to \u2018Indian Mission\u2019 without publicity and without drawing too much attention to change, to avoid if possible any constitutional issue being raised by China.\u201d&nbsp; UNQUOTE .&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">This was at a time when a full blown civil war was going on in China.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">On 15 August 1947, the day India became independent , the British mission in Lhasa (Tibet\u2019s capital) formally became the Indian mission in a shady manner.</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The last British representative in Lhasa, H.E. Richardson, became the first Indian representative there.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Richardson wrote later &nbsp;\u201cThe transition was almost imperceptible,&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">the existing staff was retained in its entirety and the only obvious change was the quiet change in the flag, without the Chinese getting even a whiff.</span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">In the case of Sikkim, &nbsp;India in&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">1949&nbsp;</span>seized the opportunity of a local uprising against the ruler to send in troops and bring the state into closer dependence as a protectorate than it had formally been under the British. &nbsp;In 1974 PM Indira Gandhi marched Indian troops into Sikkim and annexed it into India\u2014 &nbsp;so China had a valid point there , as history always repeats itself. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">In October 1950, China woke up and the Peoples\u2019 Liberation Army (PLA) vanquished a feeble Tibetan opposition in the Battle of Chamdo and thus put an end to all ongoing diplomatic negotiations on the status of Tibet.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The Indian delegation in the United Nations blocked a proposal to censure China when the Chinese forces were on their way to Lhasa. India allowed Chinese food material for its troops located near Yatung to go through Calcutta and Gangtok. &nbsp;Later, the Indian Government agreed to withdraw its military-cum-diplomatic missions in Tibet without any fuss.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The historic Sino-Indian Treaty on relations between India and the Tibet Region of China was signed in 1954. &nbsp;India gave up its rights in Tibet without seeking a quid pro quo. &nbsp;The Panch Shila was enunciated, &nbsp;which na\u00efve Nehru presumed and took for granted iron clad boundaries in an era of Hindi-Chini- bhai- bhai.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VKgE2RKRuMU/Uyf9-ZzyJQI/AAAAAAAAqbo/kuQZic-pzC4/s1600/Chinawjmjjhar_1793999f.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; font-size: 12pt;\">When Nehru visited &nbsp;China in&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">1954</span>, he showed Chou En-lai\u2019s the new political map of India, which defined the McMahon Line and the J&amp;K Johnson Line as firm borders (and not in dotted lines ) and expressed concern over corresponding Chinese maps that he found erroneous. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Chou En-lai replied that the Chinese had not yet found time to correct their old maps but that this would be done \u201cwhen the time is ripe\u201d. Relations were hunky dory or kissing terms .&nbsp;Nehru assumed this implied tacit Chinese acceptance of India\u2019s map alignments but referred to the same matter once again during Chou\u2019s 1956 visit to India.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The young Dalai Lama came to India in&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">1956&nbsp;</span>to participate in the 2,500th anniversary celebrations commemorating the Enlightenment of the Buddha but was reluctant to return home as he felt China had reneged from its promise of Tibetan autonomy. &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; Following the failed 1959 Tibetan uprising, &nbsp;the 14th Dalai Lama sought refuge in India. Nehru, allowed in the Dalai Lama and his coterie of Tibetan government officials. &nbsp;The Dalai Lama has since lived in exile in Dharamshala, in the state of Himachal Pradesh in northern India, where the Central Tibetan Administration is also established.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-iM26xnGcgxw/UIcHH666NJI/AAAAAAAAVtQ/5qeu7jWwb2g/s1600/downloadjyfm.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-iM26xnGcgxw/UIcHH666NJI/AAAAAAAAVtQ/5qeu7jWwb2g/s1600/downloadjyfm.jpg\" height=\"400\" width=\"383\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The Government of India granted Dalai Lama asylum, along with his entourage and over 100,000 refugees that followed. These events greatly disturbed the Chinese who saw this as a great Indian betrayal. This event marked a turning point in Sino-Indian relations for the worse. &nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Indian troops crossed over into Tibet to escort the Dalai Lama and party into India across the McMahon line.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">They came with their men and mules heavily laden with gold. While granting \u2018political asylum\u2019 to the Dalai Lama, the Indian government assured Peking that he would not be allowed to carry on political activities from the soil of India. As usual, this assurance proved to be a false one. The Chinese knew from the wordings and tone, that the Dalai Lama\u2019s first statement issued from India was drawn up by Indian officials .</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Their suspicions about India\u2019s intentions were fuelled by Nehru\u2019s connivance in facilitating CIA trained Tibetan refugee guerrillas to operate in Tibet and further permitting an American listening spy facility to be planted on the heights of Nanda Devi to monitor Chinese radio signals in Tibet.</span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">China now suspected that India was all the while helping the Khampa rebellion and had assisted the Dalai Lama to escape to India. The disputed border and hardening of attitudes on both sides led to several skirmishes on several border posts. &nbsp;The Government of India adopted a strategically flawed \u2018Forward Policy\u2019 of erecting isolated check posts on the border without improving &nbsp;infrastructure or the armed forces\u2019 capabilities.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Towards the end of&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">1961</span>, Mao said enough is enough, and convened a meeting of China\u2019s Central Military Commission and took personal charge of the \u2018struggle with India\u2019.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Five years later, China started the construction of the 179-km long western Tibet-Sinkiang road passing through Aksai Chin, part of J&amp;K and claimed by India. The Government of India took two and a half years to confirm this information.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-td804GaEw3s/UIcH7Zn4hUI/AAAAAAAAVtw/RcfdL7o8HTE/s1600/war1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-td804GaEw3s/UIcH7Zn4hUI/AAAAAAAAVtw/RcfdL7o8HTE/s320/war1.jpg\" height=\"448\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">CIA could have given this information to India, but they chose not to. The whole idea was to make India and China bitter enemies, and provoke them to fight a war to sow permanent seeds of mistrust.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Aksai Chin a barren stretch of land ( area 37,000 square km ) of high-altitude desert with no human habitation, was a part of the Ladakh region, which China claims it to be part of its Xinjiang autonomous region. &nbsp;The MaCartney-MacDonald line clearly puts Aksai Chin within Chinese territory.&nbsp; China invested money and effort to make the highway there.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">This new road was disclosed to the Indian Parliament &nbsp;on August 31, 1959, causing a huge uproar, the way only Indian MPs are capable of. &nbsp;Nehru\u2019s remark that \u2018not a blade of grass grows there\u2019 did not cut ice with the much agitated Opposition in Parliament, &nbsp;who cried that if there is no grass in your dang back yard , will you gift it away?.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">Nehru's thus became adamant that China must withdraw from Aksai Chin and in the process abandon the highway China made was seen by Mao as further Indian attempts to undermine China's claim to Tibet.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The border between India and Tibet had remained undefined and undemarcated when the direct rule of India by the British ended in 1947.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Vast areas in the north-east, mountainous and sparsely populated by tribes, and in the north-west, mountainous, icy and desolate, were never ever under the administration of India.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">\u201cThe great cartographic forgery,\u201d as Sourin Roy, a former deputy director, National Archives of India, pointed out, was initiated by Sir Olaf Kirkpatrick Kruuse Caroe , Governor of NWFP , and was completed under Nehru in 1954, as per Edwina\u2019s advise to Nehru, of a Forward policy .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">\u201cThe frontier from Bhutan eastwards has been clearly defined by the McMahon line which was fixed by the Simla Convention of 1914.... Our maps show that the McMahon line is our boundary and that is our boundary \u2014 map or no map.\u201d . &nbsp;Since 1938, however, the Survey of India maps were surreptitiously altered, &nbsp;showing the McMahon Line, with the word \u2018Undemarcated\u2019 imprinted on it.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The McMahon Line drawn in Shimla convention of 1914 between British Empire and Tibet was rejected by China. &nbsp;China officially claims the entire Arunachal Pradesh as its territory based on its traditional boundaries from the imperial past.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The CIA collaborated with India and Nepal in training Tibetan exiles to fight Chinese troops. Between the late 1950\u2019s and mid-1960\u2019s the US government flew hundreds of Tibetan exiles to far-flung bases in Okinawa, Guam and Colorado.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">There they were trained as guerrillas to wage war against the Chinese.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The Tibetans, many of whom were recruited from the Khamba tribe, were parachuted back into Tibet at night with sub-machine guns.
