font-size: 12pt;\">Meanwhile Mao wanted to double check political polarisations and alliances. The Chinese Ambassador to Warsaw, Wang Bingnan, was recalled from leave and hastily dispatched to Warsaw with instructions to meet his US counterpart forthwith.&nbsp; &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">On 23 June 1962, Wang Bingnan met US Ambassador Cabot at Warsaw. &nbsp;Ambassador Wang claimed that Beijing had noted US preparations in Taiwan for a landing on the mainland.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Ambassador Cabot, who was unaware of any such preparations, based on his brief from the State Department, conveyed to his Chinese interlocutor that he had been authorized to state that the US government had no intention of supporting the proposed&nbsp; GRC [Taiwan] attack on the mainland in 1962.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The Chinese breathed a huge sigh of relief for they were anticipating trouble on two widely separated fronts.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">On&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">8 October 1962</span>, Chinese leaders informed the Soviet Ambassador in Beijing that \u2018China knows that Indian forces are planning to launch a large scale attack in Sino-Indian frontier regions and if India launches an attack than we will resolutely carry out self-defence.\u2019&nbsp; &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Further, Ambassador Liu secured from Khrushchev \u2018guarantees\u2019 that if China was attacked and a China-India War ensued, the Soviets would \u2018stand together with China\u2019 .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">With the Cuba crisis in his mind and wanting China as an ally in case of a nuclear missile war with USA, in a 20 October 1962 letter, Khrushchev rebuked Nehru for failing to show \u2018due urge for reconciliation\u2019 and urged him \u2018to agree to Chinese proposals\u2019. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8mgvpROSX58/UIcG6pB5x8I/AAAAAAAAVtI/KLfgofh6hOY/s1600/imagesJHBGUYBMJ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8mgvpROSX58/UIcG6pB5x8I/AAAAAAAAVtI/KLfgofh6hOY/s400/imagesJHBGUYBMJ.jpg\" height=\"290\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">This new tough line was confirmed when MJ Desai [then Secretary General, MEA] told US Ambassador Galbraith in a meeting on 23 October 1962 that \u2018in the past few days the Soviets have taken a tough line with the Indians\u2014 including advice to settle on Chinese terms.\u2019&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The friends of VK Krishna Menon, the Soviets really had had no option as they were engrossed in a serious confrontation with the US over Cuba and badly needed Chinese support, in case of a full scale nuclear missile war with USA and UK. &nbsp;Support for India was expendable, at this hour.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">This is the reason why every nation should have its own security, instead of hanging on and hiding under somebody else\u2019s stinkin' petticoat.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">In its issue of&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">14 October 1962</span>, the Chinese People\u2019s Daily again warned Nehru : \u201cPull back from the brink of the precipice and don\u2019t use the lives of Indian troops as stakes in your gamble.\u201d &nbsp;The advice was ignored.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">It must be noted here that VK Krishna Menon &nbsp;was never privy to false promises and constant meddling by CIA. &nbsp; CIA , Rothschild and the US president hated Menon\u2019s guts. &nbsp;&nbsp;So any man with average intelligence can make out that he was not privy to the China territory nibbling process and Tibet provocations done by Nehru and IB chief Mullick.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_3n7DQAZgBc/UIcHTNfwJ_I/AAAAAAAAVtY/7QFFSEjjTeI/s1600/imagesYY64H.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_3n7DQAZgBc/UIcHTNfwJ_I/AAAAAAAAVtY/7QFFSEjjTeI/s640/imagesYY64H.jpg\" height=\"412\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">On&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">14 October 1962</span>, an editorial on People's Daily issued China's the last and final warning to India: QUOTE &nbsp;\"<i>So it seems that Mr. Nehru has made up his mind to attack the Chinese frontier guards on an even bigger scale....It is high time to shout to Mr. Nehru that the heroic Chinese troops, with the glorious tradition of resisting foreign aggression, can never be cleared by anyone from their own territory... If there are still some maniacs who are reckless enough to ignore our well-intentioned advice and insist on having another try, well, let them do so. History will pronounce its inexorable verdict... At this critical moment...we still want to appeal once more to Mr. Nehru: better rein in at the edge of the precipice and do not use the lives of Indian troops as stakes in your gamble.</i>\"UNQUOTE&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The Chinese insisted that it was India that started the conflict by following the so-called \u2018forward policy\u2019 and \u2018nibbling\u2019 at China\u2019s frontiers, and hence it was only a \u2018counter-attack\u2019 and in \u2018self-defence\u2019 to throw out Indian \u2018aggressors\u2019 from Chinese territory. &nbsp;&nbsp;In other words, it was an action designed to reclaim Chinese territory wrongly usurped by India \u2013 with American connivance , aimed to draw away Chinese forces from the sensitive Taiwan area.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">On&nbsp;</span><span style=\"color: red; font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">16 October 1962</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">, this war plan was approved, and on the 18th, the final approval was given by the Politburo for a \"self-defensive counter-attack\", &nbsp;scheduled for 20 October.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">On&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">20 October 1962</span>, at 5 AM IST, the Chinese People's Liberation Army launched two massive onslaughts , 1000 kilometres apart. &nbsp;Three Chinese Regiments, 154, 155 and 157 [equivalent to Indian Brigades], all battle-hardened veterans of the Korean War transferred from across the Taiwan Straits since June 1962, attacked Indian positions across the Namka Chu defended by a single brigade and overran them.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Similar attacks were launched simultaneously on all Indian positions both in the Western and Eastern sectors with overwhelming force.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">This attack was a well planned move and it coincided with the Cuban Missile Crisis, which made sure that USA and Russians will NOT bother to intervene\u2014or even give a patient ear.</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The Cuban missile crisis was a 13-day confrontation between the Soviet Union and Cuba on one side and the United States on the other. The crisis occurred in October 1962, during the Cold War from October 16\u201328, 1962 (naval blockade of Cuba ended November 20, 1962) .</span>&nbsp;</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The Soviet government secretly began to build bases in Cuba for a number of medium-range and intermediate-range ballistic nuclear missiles (MRBMs and IRBMs) with the ability to strike most of the continental United States. In addition to nuclear-armed ballistic missiles, the Soviet Union had deployed 100 tactical nuclear weapons to Cuba, and the local Soviet commander there could have launched these weapons without additional codes or commands from Moscow.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UmH7pn6nqdU/Uyf-V9CBNWI/AAAAAAAAqb4/_3if0DyyfR4/s1600/Photo+Division+DPR+Mm+hjOD+Image+No+04.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-UmH7pn6nqdU/Uyf-V9CBNWI/AAAAAAAAqb4/_3if0DyyfR4/s1600/Photo+Division+DPR+Mm+hjOD+Image+No+04.JPG\" height=\"433\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The U.S. air strike and invasion that were scheduled for the third week of the confrontation would likely have triggered a nuclear response against American ships and troops, and perhaps even Miami. The resulting war might have led to the deaths of 100 million Americans, and a deadly retaliation by USA .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">In the western theatre, the Chinese PLA sought to expel Indian forces from the Chip Chap valley in Aksai China while in the eastern theatre, the PLA sought to capture both banks of the Namka Chu river. &nbsp;The Chinese cut the Indian telephone lines, preventing the Indian defenders from making contact with their headquarters. To be frank these are all basics.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The Chinese troops launched a three-pronged attack on Tawang, Arunachal Pradesh which the Indians evacuated without any resistance. &nbsp;The entire NEFA (North East Frontier Agency), now called Arunachal Pradesh was Gen Kaul's domain. &nbsp;On his first day of assignment, Gen Kaul flew to Lumpu in great style and then trekked like a commando to Namkachu valley. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">He was the first General officer to visit the valley. &nbsp;Gen Kaul \u201creportedly\u201d fell ill during the assignment and was deported to New Delhi and the IV Corps was wiped out when a strong enemy force raided the camp.&nbsp; The battle with China in 1962, in the NEFA, is also known as the Battle of Namkachu.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">There is ample evidence today from doctors that Nehru\u2019s relative and blue eyed boy Gen Kaul &nbsp;was not as sick as he said. &nbsp;Gen Kaul\u2019s famous last words before he came back to Delhi was to tell the brigade commander before leaving: \u201cIts your battle now\u201d. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">When General Kaul reached 7th Brigade at Tawang, he wanted to inspect the front lines himself. Because of the altitude, he was already exhausted. &nbsp;No 4 legged pack animals were available. &nbsp;So a two legged local porter manfully carried our dear Gen Kaul off to the front like a sack of potatoes. &nbsp;Needless to say all onlookers were amused.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: large;\"><b><i>Vidi Vini Vizi</i>, or was it so? &nbsp;&nbsp;</b></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: large;\"><b><br /></b></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>It could be-- &nbsp; I came, &nbsp;I spied ( with mE little eye ) , I scooted ( by piggy back ride ).</b></span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Indian Army was not ready to take on the Chinese. &nbsp;Very few Indian soldiers had operated on freezing mountain areas. &nbsp;The troops were using obsolete weapons unsuitable for mountain warfare and bullets were in short supply. &nbsp;Most of the time the Chinese were outside Indian rifle range.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The Chinese were well supplied as they had stocked supplies in Tibet and their soldiers were well acquainted with mountain warfare.</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The Indian soldiers, did not even have enough winter clothing and shoes.&nbsp; There was no road network. The supplies and reinforcements for the troops were sent most by air.</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Indian<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;troops were short on artillery and ammunition and the artillery pieces they had was very often immobile in the mountains. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Lieutenant General B M Kaul, had never commanded an active fighting outfit in his entire life and he was to command one now.</span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The majority of Chinese forces had advanced to sixteen kilometres south of the control line prior to the conflict. &nbsp;Four days of fighting were followed by a three-week lull. Zhou ordered the troops to stop advancing as he attempted to negotiate with Nehru a last time .&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">On&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">October 24 1962</span>,&nbsp; Beijing offered a ceasefire and Chinese withdrawal on the express condition that India agreed to open negotiations. &nbsp;Nehru refused the offer even before the text was officially received. &nbsp;Both sides built up over the next three weeks and the Indians launched a local counterattack on November 15, arousing in India fresh expectations of total victory, what with our newspapers giving rosy accounts of Indian bravery and relentless assaults.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Zhou had sent Nehru a letter, proposing a negotiated settlement of the boundary, that both sides disengage and withdraw twenty kilometres from present lines of actual control. &nbsp;After Zhou received Nehru's letter (rejecting Zhou's proposal), the fighting resumed on the eastern theatre on&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">14 November 1962&nbsp;</span>(Nehru's birthday).</span><o:p></o:p></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">On&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">17 November 1962</span>, the Chinese troops in this second campaign reached the borders of Assam, occupied the entire disputed territory of the NEFA and again halted. The Indian government was seized with panic, almost wrote off Assam as lost.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Mao in a master stroke declared unilateral ceasefire on&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">November 20, 1962</span>, immediately after the resolution of crisis in the Cuba.&nbsp; Many units of the once crack Indian 4th Division dissolved into rout without giving battle and by November 20 1962, there was no organised Indian resistance anywhere in the disputed territories. This time a shaken up Nehru tacitly accepted.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Zhou's ceasefire declaration stated,<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">QUOTE<i>&nbsp;\u201cBeginning from&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;\">21 November 1962</span>, the Chinese frontier guards will cease fire along the entire Sino-Indian border. &nbsp;Beginning from 1 December 1962, the Chinese frontier guards will withdraw to positions 20 kilometres behind the line of actual control which existed between China and India on 7 November 1959. In the eastern sector, although the Chinese frontier guards have so far been fighting on Chinese territory north of the traditional customary line, they are prepared to withdraw from their present positions to the north of the illegal McMahon Line, and to withdraw twenty kilometres back from that line. In the middle and western sectors, the Chinese frontier guards will withdraw twenty kilometres from the line of actual control.\u201d</i>UNQUOTE<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">The Chinese withdrew twelve miles north of the McMahon line and returned captured Indian soldiers whom they had treated well with their small arms.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">In the meantime the Indian army chief, General Thapar, resigned. &nbsp;The defence minister, Krishna Menon (Nehru\u2019s close friend ), was made a scapegoat by all those who hated him.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">VK Krishna Menon, the \u201cterror from the East\u201d who gave the white man a massive inferiority complex, was forced to resign by USA as a pre-condition for military aid and by Rothschild for financial aid.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">This was their way of getting even with all the mental lashes and intellectual bleeding they had to lump. There was NOT a single English speaking white man on this planet, who could better VK Krishna Menon&nbsp; in a debate on any political subject.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt;\">After his famous nine-hour speech on Kashmir at the UN Security Council in 1957, during which he lambasted both the US and Britain, the British delegate, Sir Pierson Dixon, laughingly told him, \u201cNo hard feelings, Krishna, we have a very thick skin.\u201d &nbsp; \u201cI know, Pierson,\u201d retorted Menon, \u201cthat\u2019s why you Britons made the best boots in the world\u201d.</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">Without batting an eyelid, &nbsp;Menon returned the lecture and concluded it with a question to the host: &nbsp;\u201c But tell me, is it true that you are a bastard??\u201d &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; Bombay\u2019s chief minister, ( CIA and Rothschild approved ) , became India\u2019s new defence minister, &nbsp;to make sure India does NOT drift to the Soviet camp.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; All of them could NOT have lost their bullets , right?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">The 1962 War has left gaping wound in the Indian psyche. The political and military leadership sacrificed officers and soldiers under them despite knowing that the army was not prepared to take on the Chinese forces in a terrain where we were logistically weak and did not have proper supply lines.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 24px;\">&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">At the same time, I would call this war as a blessing in disguise.&nbsp; India gained many benefits from the 1962 conflict. The border between Sikkim and China, though, is still not fully demarcated.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;\">China had been active in Aksai Chin for over a decade before 1962. &nbsp;India was aware of Chinese activity there from 1951. In 1957, Beijing's road building activities could not be ignored any longer, and India sent patrols to the area. It would be the beginning of the India-China conflict that would culminate in 1962.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">Gen Kaul although Sandhurst-trained for infantry service , he pussy footed his army&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">career</span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">&nbsp;using his Nehru connections,&nbsp;without serving on any front line and ended it in a humble and obscure post in public relations, but all the time enjoying ZE good life. &nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; When you convert people from other religions with missionaries aggressively harvesting by shoving sops down hapless throats, conscience takes a back seat.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A comfortable house and\nwealth is a great source of happiness. It ranks only after good health which springs\nout of happiness anchored by good conscience.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Betrayal of trust and\ningratitude is &nbsp;common for men with no\nconscience.&nbsp; A guilty conscience needs no\naccuser. There is pillow as hard as a guilty conscience.<o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Conscience is what\nmakes you behave well behind closed doors or when nobody is looking...</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Numerous case studies\nof brain damage have shown that damage to areas of the brain (such as the\nanterior prefrontal cortex) results in the reduction or elimination of\ninhibitions, with a corresponding radical change in behaviour. When the damage\noccurs to adults, they may still be able to perform moral reasoning.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-DprVPDTGBXc/UIMGiBed3VI/AAAAAAAAVlM/yJcUKe6xSy4/s1600/ssxc.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-DprVPDTGBXc/UIMGiBed3VI/AAAAAAAAVlM/yJcUKe6xSy4/s1600/ssxc.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Conscience\nan aspect of extended consciousness beyond survival-related dispositions . Conscience\nis a gift of crisis--- It tells you the right thing to do when you don't have\ntime to figure it all out. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Conscience\nthinks in a flash, in terms of metaphor, feelings, pictures, and the spatial\nwhole and doesn't fit neatly into the cause-and-effect model. Your conscience\nwill not force you to do things that are truly wrong for yourself or other\npeople in contradiction with the laws of the universe.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">We cannot command our conscience\nto use it at will. It just surfaces spontaneously when certain circumstances\nare present\u2014it suddenly appears as a feeling. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Conscience extrapolates larger truths . Use it\nas a guide always, never ignore it.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times New Roman, serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">We in India know the meaning of conscience -- in 4300 BC, when Lord Sri-Ram was sent away to the forest for 14 years in exile ( cheated in a dice game wager ) his step-brother Bharat , whose mother Kaikeyi did the foul spadework , &nbsp;kept Rama's shoes on the throne , till the exile period was over. &nbsp;Prince Bharat ran to the forest to seek out King Sri Ram and&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">apologize</span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;on behalf of his mother.</span></span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; It is a powerful vasodilator with a short half-life\nof a few seconds in the blood. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Nitric oxide controls\nblood flow in our body.&nbsp; It controls our\nvascular resistance , the blood pressure . Do not count the 1\u2019s.)</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif;\">When the first number to the right of the 1 in any row is a prime number, all numbers in that row are divisible by that prime number</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif;\">The Fibonacci Series is found in Pascal\u2019s Triangle.</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif;\">Pascal\u2019s Triangle, is formed by starting with an apex of 1. Every number below in the triangle is the sum of the two numbers diagonally above it to the left and the right, with positions outside the triangle counting as zero.</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif;\">The numbers on diagonals of the Pascalstriangle add to the Fibonacci series</span><br /><span style=\"color: red;\"><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif;\">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XMriWTvPXHI&amp;pbjreload=10</span></span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif;\">The Fibonacci numbers are--</span><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif;\">0, 1, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8, 13, ... This algorithm is known in mathematics as the Sieve of Eratosthenes--inherent in sruti verses of Vedas<br /><br />In mathematics, the sieve of Eratosthenes one of a number of prime number sieves, is a simple, ancient algorithm for finding all prime numbers up to any given limit.<br /><br />It does so by iteratively marking as composite, i.e., not prime, the multiples of each prime, starting with the multiples of 2. The multiples of a given prime are generated starting from that prime, as a sequence of numbers with the same difference, equal to that prime, between consecutive numbers.<br /><br />This is the sieve's key distinction from using trial division to sequentially test each candidate number for divisibility by each prime.<br /><br />MY REVELATIONS NOW JUMP TO&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red;
